BRIEF OF COMPANY
It all started with a young Dhaka University graduate on vacation walking into an advertisement agency in Karachi. The next thing he knows, he has been appointed as an English copywriter for East Asiatic in Dhaka. Growing through the ranks, he finally bought East Asiatic when the government put it up for sale after the liberation war. He changed the name to Asiatic Marketing Communications Ltd. And, the rest is history.
